let api = ea.getExcalidrawAPI();

const svgToBase64 = (svg) => {
  return `data:image/svg+xml;base64,${btoa(
      unescape(encodeURIComponent(svg.replaceAll("&nbsp;", " "))),
  )}`;
};
function hasPropertiesChanged(a, b) {
  return Math.abs(a.width - b.width) > 0.5 || Math.abs(a.height - b.height) > 0.5 || a?.customData?.codeHighlight != b?.customData?.codeHighlight || a.text != b.text;//不能用width不相等，否则双击后再点击空白，drawimage不会变化到canvas
}
function loadHljs(doAfterLoaded) {
  let script = document.createElement("script");
  script.id = "hljs"
  script.onload = function () {
    if (doAfterLoaded)
      doAfterLoaded();
  };
  // script.src =
  //   "https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/highlight.js/11.9.0/highlight.min.js";
  script.textContent = hljsContent;
  ea.targetView.contentEl.appendChild(script);

  script = document.createElement("script");
  script.id = "hljs-languages"
  script.textContent = verilog;
  ea.targetView.contentEl.appendChild(script);
  
  return script
}
window.customData = window.customData || {}
window.customData.codeMap = window.customData.codeMap || new Map();

console.log("drawElementOnCanvasHook")
window.drawElementOnCanvasHook = function(element, context, renderConfig, rc) {
  if (element?.customData?.areaLink?.viewBox) {
    // console.log("drawElementOnCanvasHook")
    context.clearRect(0, 0, element.width, element.height);
    const imageCache = renderConfig.imageCache.get(element.fileId)
    if (!imageCache) return false
    const img = imageCache?.image
    const viewBox = element.customData.areaLink.viewBox
  
    context.drawImage(
      img,
      viewBox[0],
      viewBox[1],
      viewBox[2],
      viewBox[3],
      0,
      0,
      viewBox[2],
      viewBox[3],
    );
    return true
  }
  if (element?.customData?.codeHighlight) {
    const hljsDom = document.getElementById("hljs")
    if (!hljsDom) {
      loadHljs()
    }
    const cache = window.customData.codeMap.get(element.id)
    let image;
    if (!cache || (cache && hasPropertiesChanged(cache.element, element))) {
      const lines = element.text.split("\n")
      const codes = []
      const language = element.customData.codeHighlight.language
      lines.forEach(line => {
        codes.push(hljs.highlight(line, {language: language}))
      })

      var div = document.createElement('div');
      div.className = `hljs language-${language}`;
      div.innerHTML = codes.reduce((sum, code) => {
        sum += code.value
        sum += "</br>"
        return sum
      }, "")
      div.style.width = `${element.width+20}px`;
      div.style.height = `${element.height+20}px`;
      div.style.fontSize = `${element.fontSize}px`;
      div.style.whiteSpace = "pre-wrap"
      div.style.padding = "10px 10px 10px 10px"
      div.style.fontFamily = ExcalidrawLib.getFontFamilyString({fontFamily:element.fontFamily})
      div.style.lineHeight = element.lineHeight;
      div.style.boxSizing = "content-box";
      div.style.letterSpacing = "initial";
      div.style.textWrap = "nowrap";
      const xml = new XMLSerializer().serializeToString(div);
      let fontDef;
      if (element?.customData?.codeHighlight?.embedFont) {
        fontDef = ExcalidrawLib.getCSSFontDefinition2(element.fontFamily)
      }
      // var el = document.createElement('div');
      const svg = `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="${element.width+20}" height="${element.height+20}">
      <style>${ea.tools.codeHighlight.style[element?.customData?.codeHighlight?.style]}
      </style>
      <foreignObject x="0" y="0" width="100%" height="100%">
      ${xml}
      </foreignObject>
      ${fontDef ? `<defs><style>${fontDef}</style></defs>` : ""}
      </svg>`
      const base64 = svgToBase64(svg)
      // el.innerHTML = `<img src="${base64}"/>`;
      // image = el.firstChild;
      image = new Image()
      image.src = base64;

      window.customData.codeMap.set(element.id, {//set cache, wait to complete
        element: element,
        svg: svg,
        image: image
      })
      if (!image.complete) {//sync version maybe not complete https://stackoverflow.com/questions/33266564/how-to-synchronously-draw-an-image-to-a-canvas
        image.onload = async () => {
          await ea?.tools?.updateSceneByZoom?.()
        }
        // image = cache?.image || image
      }
    } else {
      image = cache.image
    }
    context.drawImage(
      image,
      -10,
      -10,
      element.width+20,
      element.height+20
    )

    return true
  }
  if (element.customData?.filter?.inner) {
    // context.save()
    context.filter = element?.customData?.filter?.inner;
  } 
  if (element?.customData?.wavedrom) {
    let script = document.getElementById("wavedrom")
    if(!script) {
        script = document.createElement("script");
        script.id = "wavedrom"
        script.type = "text/javascript";
        script.textContent = wavedrom_js;
        
        document.body.appendChild(script);
        script = document.createElement("script");
        script.id = "wavedrom-default"
        script.type = "text/javascript";
        script.textContent = default_js;
        document.body.appendChild(script);
    }
    const cache = window.customData.codeMap.get(element.id)
    let image;
    if (!cache || (cache && hasPropertiesChanged(cache.element, element))) {
      content = element?.rawText
      if (!content) return

      script = document.getElementById("InputJSON_0")
      if(!script) {
          script = document.createElement("script");
          script.id = "InputJSON_0"
          script.type = "WaveDrom"
          document.body.appendChild(script);
      }
      script.innerHTML = content
      window.WaveDrom.ProcessAll()
      let WaveDrom_Display_0 = document.querySelector("#WaveDrom_Display_0")
      let svg = WaveDrom_Display_0.firstChild

      var serializer = new XMLSerializer();
      var svgString = serializer.serializeToString(svg);


      const base64 = svgToBase64(svgString)
      image = new Image()
      image.src = base64;

      window.customData.codeMap.set(element.id, {//set cache, wait to complete
        element: element,
        svg: svgString,
        image: image
      })
      if (!image.complete) {
        image.onload = async () => {
          await ea?.tools?.updateSceneByZoom?.()
        }
      }
    } else {
      image = cache.image
    }
    context.drawImage(
      image,
      -10,
      -10,
      element.width+20,
      element.height+20
    )

  }
  return false
}
